


// 数组排序[大->小]
void sort(int nums[]){
    for (int i=9; i>0; i–){
        for (int j=i-1; j>=0; j–){
            if (nums[i] > nums[j]){
                int temp = nums[j];
                nums[j] = nums[i];
                nums[i] = temp;
            }
        }

}

}

// 数组去重
int unique(int nums[]){
int U = new int [10];
for (int i=1; i<10; i++){
U[0] = nums[0];
if (nums[i] == nums[i-1]){
U[i] = -1;
}
else{ U[i] = nums[i];}
}
return U;
}

// 数组打印
void print(int nums[10]){
for (int i=0; i<10; i++){
cout << nums[i];
}
}

// 结果打印
void print_array(int nums[], int person_num[]){
for (int i=0; i<10; i++){
if (nums[i] >= 0)
for (int j=0; j<10; j++){
if (person_num[j] == nums[i]){
cout << “Person “<<(j+1)<<” : ate “<< nums[i]<< “ pancakes”<<endl;
}
}
}
}

int main(){
int nums [10];
int person_num [10];
cout << “Specify the number of pancake for the Person x: \n”;
for (int i=0; i<10; i++){
cout << “Person “<< (i+1)<< “: “;
cin >> nums[i];
person_num[i] = nums[i];
}
sort(nums);
int *U = unique(nums);
//print(U);
print_array(U, person_num);  
    delete U;   
    return 0;
}
